"THE IDOL" must have been inspired by the Jabba the Hut & Slave Leia scene from "Return of the Jedi". Only the most hopelessly obsequious woke enabler would ever consider the bloated and boring weak end to be sexy and seductive. Watch him trying to rock a trenchcoat. It's laughable yet we're supposed to think he's slick. It's easy to be a hustler when the bleeding heart big shots have been brainwashed into believing that they owe you stardom. Anybody else spouting such cheesy porn talk would have been rightfully dismissed as a clown pervert. It must be sweet to have the system so thoroughly rigged on your behalf that the world is forced to accept the preposterous premise that the unwatchable weak end is some badass super stud, lest we be found guilty of violating some PC dogma.  Part of the time, 'THE IDOL" wants to be a satire poking fun at the usual show biz phonies and flunkies. But then it pretends to shine a harsh spotlight on the sleaziness of the music industry, while at the same time celebrating the sleaze. Back in the seventies, nobody cared about the sleaze because the music was great. But then MTV and madonna took over and the quality of the music became irrelevant. The MTV boom era faded away a long time ago, but the music industry is still stuck in the tired and tiresome post-madonna paradigm of bubblegum narcissism. Why? A TV series that answers that question would be worth watching.   http://www.reverbnation.com/QANEIDA

I've got a crazy, but absolutely 100% true story about my families weekend that everyone has to hear. Me and my wife and our 5 children, went to a beach resort for the weekend. We were having such a good time. We decided to go horseback riding, and that's when things started going south. Literally. Read on.   My wife was riding a horse that, well let's just say it wasn't the smoothest ride one has ever had on a horse. Yeah it was bouncing her up and down in that saddle pretty good.
